<div class="article-text wide" id="js-article-text">
<h1>For the first time ever...Queen: Ten great hits from the sensational rock band in today's The Mail on Sunday<br/></h1><p><br/></p><p class="byline-section author-section byline-plain">By

<a class="author" href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Mail+on+Sunday+Reporter" rel="nofollow">Mail on Sunday Reporter</a>
<br/><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
<span class="article-timestamp-label">Updated:</span>
  05:12 EST, 19 June 2009
</span>
<br/><div id="articleIconLinksContainer">
<ul>
<li class="share-facebook"></li>
<li class="share-twitter"></li>
<li class="share-pinterest"></li>
<li class="share-gplus">
<span class="g-interactivepost" data-calltoactionlabel="VIEW" data-calltoactionurl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html" data-clientid="746589970956-e10ciaf67a1id9ggu75ph3ds0sthn7j6.apps.googleusercontent.com" data-contentdeeplinkid="/pages" data-contenturl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html" data-cookiepolicy="single_host_origin" data-prefilltext="For the first time ever...Queen: Ten great hits from the sensational rock band in today's The Mail on Sunday">
<a></a>
</span>
</li>
<li class="share-email">
<a class="js-email" data-ajax-refresh-everytime="true" data-modal-id="email-modal-overlay" data-modal-type="email-overlay" data-on-mobile="mailto:?subject=For the first time ever...Queen: Ten great hits from the sensational rock band in today's The Mail on Sunday&amp;body=http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html" data-placement="top" data-target="/emailArticle.html?id=1169307" data-toggle="modal" href="#email" title="Email to a friend"></a>
</li>
<li class="share-icons" id="shareLinkTop">
<a class="js-sl share-link" href="#socialLinks"></a>
<script type="text/javascript">
          var twitterVia = 'DailyMailCeleb';
          DM.later('bundle', function(){
            DM.has('shareLinkTop', 'shareLinks', {
                    'id': '1169307',
                    'title': 'For the first time ever...Queen: Ten great hits from the sensational rock band in today\'s The Mail on Sunday',
                    'url': 'http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html',
                    'eTwitterStatus': ' http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html via @' + twitterVia,
                    'articleChannelFollowButton': 'DailyMailCeleb',
                    'isChannel': false,
	        'hideEmail': true,
                    'placement': 'top',
                    'anchor': 'tl'});
          });
      </script>

<a class="comments-count home" href="/tvshowbiz/article-1169307/For-time--Queen-Ten-great-hits-sensational-rock-band-todays-The-Mail-Sunday.html#comments"> <span></span>
<p class="count-number"></p>
<p class="count-text">View <br> comments</br></p>
</a>
<script>
        DM.later('bundle', function(){
            DMS.Article.init('top');
        });
    </script>
</div>
<br/></p><div class="floatRHS">
<img alt="fREDDIE mERCURY" class="blkBorder" height="574" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2009/04/17/article-1169307-045FB14D000005DC-963_306x574.jpg" width="306"/>
</div>
<p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Today The Mail on Sunday brings you another exclusive musical world first. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Inside your copy you’ll find an amazing free CD by Queen – one of the greatest-ever supergroups. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Queen have never before allowed their music to be used in a collaboration with a newspaper, but founder members Brian May and Roger Taylor have worked with The Mail on Sunday to produce this very special album. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">The CD features ten full Queen tracks, including Killer Queen, Don’t Stop Me Now and the fantastic anthem We Will Rock You, all sung by Freddie Mercury, the iconic superstar who tragically died in 1991. <br/></font></p><h2><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">'We wrote for the common man': Scroll down for our exclusive interview with Brian May</font></h2><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">His extraordinary voice is complemented by Brian May’s exhilarating
guitar, Roger Taylor’s storming drumming and John Deacon’s rock-solid
bass. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Queen’s music has gained a new generation of fans
through the hugely successful musical We Will Rock You, which features
all their greatest hits woven into a story written by Ben Elton. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">The musical began in the West End in 2002 and has played to packed houses around the world ever since. <br/></font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">As bonus tracks on this album you’ll also get four fantastic Queen songs performed by the original cast.</font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">There are more details about this unique Queen CD in today's The Mail on
Sunday, but if you want to be absolutely sure of getting your hands on
it, you can reserve yours now by filling in the coupon in the paper and
giving it to your newsagent.</font></p><p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Queen and The Mail on Sunday will rock you today!</font></p><p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Listen to We Will Rock You here:</font></p><div class="moduleFull" id="ext-gen4032">  																																																																																<a class="namedLink" name="video"></a><div class="item">

<p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><br/></font></p><div class="clear"> </div><div class="clear"> </div><span style="font-weight: bold;"><br/></span><h2><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">Angella Johnson's exclusive interview with Brian May</font></h2><p>From
the opening bars of anthems such as Don’t Stop Me Now and Killer Queen,
their music is instantly recognisable. Supergroup Queen have been one
of rock’s most successful, influential and popular bands – with total
record sales of more than 300million. </p><p>Now, to mark the 30th
anniversary this year of their first recorded live album, Live Killers,
The Mail on Sunday brings you another exclusive musical world first.</p><p>Inside
your copy of the paper this weekend you’ll find a fantastic free CD
featuring many of the original tracks from the Queen album fans often
describe as their best ever.</p><p>Queen have never before allowed
their music to be used in a collaboration with a newspaper, but founder
members Brian May and Roger Taylor have worked with The Mail on Sunday
to produce this very special and collectable album. </p><p>There are
ten full Queen tracks featuring hits such as Killer Queen, Don’t Stop
Me Now and, of course, the drum and guitar classic We Will Rock You.</p>
<p>They are all sung by the band’s flamboyant and much-loved frontman,
Freddie Mercury – the iconic superstar who tragically died in 1991. His
extraordinary voice is complemented by May’s exhilarating guitar,
Taylor’s storming drumming and John Deacon’s rock-solid bass.</p>
<div class="clear"> </div>
<img alt="True showmen: Freddie Mercury and Brian May at one of their live performances" class="blkBorder" height="400" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2009/04/18/article-1169307-04823523000005DC-115_634x400.jpg" width="634"/>
<p class="imageCaption">True showmen: Freddie Mercury and Brian May at one of their live performances</p>
<p>In a rare interview, Brian admits that the group were inspired from
the outset by the enthusiasm of their live audiences, who loved to clap
and sing along to their songs.</p><p>‘We wrote for the common man,’ he
says. ‘About how we felt, our dreams and frustrations. That’s why they
identified so much with us.</p><p>‘We are known for our anthem songs
but we didn’t start out that way. In the beginning we wanted people to
sit up and listen, because we thought we had something important to
say. But they wanted to participate. In the end we decided not to fight
it, but rather to enjoy and even encourage it.’</p><p>He recalls that the words and music for We Will Rock You came to him one morning after a particularly raucous concert.</p>
<p>‘We played a gig at Bingley Hall near Birmingham. It was a popular
venue at the time. It was a big sweaty barn and that night it was
packed with a particularly vocal crowd. They were definitely drowning
us out with their enthusiasm.</p><p>‘I remember that even after we left the stage they didn’t stop
singing – loudly. They sang You’ll Never Walk Alone, which is very
emotional. Quite a choking thing really. I certainly found it
inspirational.</p>
<p>‘Later that night back at our hotel I said to the
others, “That was great. So what should we do to continue generating
that kind of energetic response?” </p>
<p>‘I woke up with the We Will Rock You lyrics in my head and had it written in about 10 minutes. </p>
<div class="floatRHS">
<img alt="Rock royalty: Queen in their heyday" class="blkBorder" height="469" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2009/04/18/article-1169307-01EC3A8F0000044D-100_306x469.jpg" width="306"/>
<p class="imageCaption">Rock royalty: Queen in their heyday</p></div><p>‘I
have hundreds of versions of We Will Rock You on my iTunes. Hardly a
day goes by without people asking if they can use the song, especially
for a military purpose. Which is somewhat ironic because I’m really
anti-war.’</p><p>We Are The Champions, the power ballad written by
Mercury, is another that May says was built on audience response. ‘We
wanted to get the crowds waving and singing. It’s very unifying and
positive. People love it because it’s so uplifting. </p><p>‘Although
much of our music was created using multi-layered arrangements and
vocal harmonies – which work especially well in the recording studio –
we were into making our concerts musical events. </p><p>‘Live performances brought out the best in us, especially Freddie, who was such a showman.’ </p><p>Unusually for a band, all four members have written songs that went to No1 in the charts. </p><p>This might have been a major factor in the longevity of their unity and friendship. </p><p>Brian
says: ‘We all contributed songs to the albums and we all had successes.
Even though most people think it was Freddie and I who wrote most of
the songs, everyone had an input in each track.</p><p>‘That was why we
decided in 1989, after our 10th album, that all future outputs would be
under the Queen banner and we would all be credited for each song.’</p><p>Queen’s
music has survived and prospered for nearly 40 years and their songs
have been widely used in television commercials and at sporting events.</p><p>It
is testimony to their enduring popularity that, according to The
Guinness Book Of World Records, Queen albums have enjoyed 27 years on
the UK album charts – longer than any other musical act.</p><p>Their
1985 Live Aid performance was voted the best live rock performance of
all time in an industry poll. And their music has recently gained a new
generation of fans through the hugely successful musical We Will Rock
You, featuring all their great hits woven into a story written by Ben
Elton. </p><p>The musical began in the West End in 2002 and has been
playing to packed houses around the world ever since. It has become the
longest-running musical at London’s Dominion Theatre, overtaking the
previous record holder, Grease.</p><p>Four bonus Queen tracks, performed by the original cast of the musical, are included in our CD.</p><p>‘The
success of Rock You has been very satisfying for me personally,’ Brian
adds. ‘From 1986 we had wanted to do a musical. Freddie was especially
keen, but the initial proposal to do a script of our story as Queen
seemed too predictable and dreary, so we dropped it. </p><p>‘It was
only through my friendship with Ben Elton that the present show came
about. He suggested we create a futuristic plot on which to hang the
songs and it’s worked very well. Every time I go into the Dominion
Theatre the place is full, which is amazing, and the fact people come
back time and again even more so.</p><p>‘The show’s continued popularity lies in the fact that there is always something new to see. </p><p>‘With
each company we have new singers and that helps to keep the event
fresh. More than three million people have seen the London performance.
</p><p>‘It’s a great night out and, like our music, great escapism for all.’</p><p>Queen and The Mail on Sunday will rock you today! <br/></p><div class="clear"><br/></div><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;"><br/>Killer Queen Live CD: Track Listing<br/><br style="font-weight: bold;"/></font><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">1 We Will Rock You  (Fast Version) (Live)</font><br/><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">2 Let Me Entertain You (Live)<br/>3 Killer Queen (Live)<br/>4 Bicycle Race (Live)<br/>5 I'm In Love With My Car (Live)<br/>6 Get Down, Make Love (Live)<br/></font><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">7 Now I'm Here (Live)</font><br/><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">8 '39 (Live)</font><br/><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">9 Keep Yourself Alive (Live)</font><br/><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">10 Don't Stop Me Now (Live)</font><span style="font-weight: bold;"><br/></span><br/><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-style: italic;">Bonus tracks from the London cast recording of We Will Rock You<br/><br/></font><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">11 Somebody To Love (Live)<br/>12 I Want To Break Free (Live)<br/>13 A Kind Of Magic (Live)</font><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;"><br style="font-weight: bold;"/></font><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">14 No-One But You (Only The Good Die Young) (Live)</font><span style="font-weight: bold;"><br/><br/></span><p>
<img alt="Queen" class="blkBorder" height="615" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2009/04/11/article-1169307-00491FDD00000258-777_634x615.jpg" width="634"/>
</p><p class="imageCaption"><font style="font-size: 1.1em;">Rock Legends: Queen’s music has gained a new generation of fans through the hugely successful musical We Will Rock You</font></p><br/>
